[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbranch [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-, [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m-, and [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte sequences[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m checks available output buffer space via `if [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[33m...[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Leave the rest of the branches unchanged so they continue to use their [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting space checks and error-reporting logic.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification and Preservation of Functionality  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Adding `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out < [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;` for the single-byte case brings it in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline with the other branches’ buffer-space validation, directly preventing the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m-byte overflow.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Breaking out of the conversion loop when no space is available causes [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mUTF32ToUTF8 to return the number of bytes successfully written so far [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XML_ENC_ERR_SPACE` if none[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which is already how multi-byte branches handle [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer exhaustion.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change does not affect the semantics of multi-byte encoding or the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresulting byte sequences, and it does not alter harness, fuzzing, or utility code. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mExisting tests and functionality around XML/HTML parsing remain intact.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigations  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The only side effect is that extremely tight buffers now properly signal space[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexhaustion instead of overflowing; callers relying on subtle over-reads/over-writes[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mnone should exist[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m would notice an `ERR_SPACE` return instead.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - To mitigate, re-run the full libxml2 regression suite to confirm no behavior [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanges beyond preventing the overflow.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verification  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rebuild with AddressSanitizer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor similar[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and re-run the fuzzer; the one-byte[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap-buffer-overflow in `UTF32ToUTF8` should be eliminated.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Execute existing unit tests for encoding routines to confirm correct [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmulti-byte behavior.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. No Changes to Harness or Tests  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fix touches only `encoding.c` in the core library.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzzing harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`fuzz/html.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and existing test files remain untouched.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No external dependencies or other modules are modified.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root-Cause Analysis[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The heap-buffer-overflow in UTF32ToUTF8 stems from missing bounds checks [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore writing [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes to the `out` buffer. The attempted patch correctly [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroduced `outend = out + *outlen` and length-guarded cases but left an unbalanced[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomment block around the surrogate-pair logic, causing a stray `*[0m[35m/[0m[39m` and compilation[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfailure.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fix must [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m balance or remove the legacy comment, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m insert explicit [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspace checks before every multi-byte write [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m, and [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplement correct UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m encoding for surrogate pairs under those checks.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Detailed Steps to Implement the Patch[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Prologue Changes[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - At the top of `UTF32ToUTF8` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter retrieving `*inlen`, `*outlen`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclare:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        unsigned char *outend = out + *outlen;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This gives a fixed upper bound for all subsequent buffer writes.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Guarding [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-, [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-, and [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m-byte Branches[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - For `c < [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out < [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = c;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        in += [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m; out += [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - For `c < [0m[1;36m0x800[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out < [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc >> [0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m   | [0m[1;36m0xC0[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc & [0m[1;36m0x3F[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m | [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        in += [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m; out += [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - For `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mc & [0m[1;36m0xF800[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0xD800[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m3[0m[39m-byte[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out < [0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m =  [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc >> [0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m        | [0m[1;36m0xE0[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mc >>  [0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m & [0m[1;36m0x3F[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m| [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m][0m[39m =  [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc        & [0m[1;36m0x3F[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m| [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        in += [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m; out += [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In each case, if the guard fails, the loop breaks out with `ret == [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXML_ENC_ERR_SPACE`.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Surrogate-Pair [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Branch[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Remove the legacy comment block entirely or close it properly before code, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meliminating the stray `*[0m[35m/[0m[39m`.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - After validating `c` and `d`, compute the full code point:[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        c = [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mc & [0m[1;36m0x3FF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m << [0m[1;36m10[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m | [0m[1;39m([0m[39md & [0m[1;36m0x3FF[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m0x10000[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Guard space:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutend - out < [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc >> [0m[1;36m18[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m        | [0m[1;36m0xF0[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mc >> [0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m & [0m[1;36m0x3F[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m| [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mc >>  [0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m & [0m[1;36m0x3F[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m| [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        out[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m][0m[39m =  [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc        & [0m[1;36m0x3F[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m| [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        in += [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m; out += [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Ensure no stray comment terminators are left unbalanced.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Post-Loop Handling[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - After the loop, update:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        *outlen = out - outstart;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        *inlen  = in  - instart;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        return ret;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This logic already exists; ensure it remains unchanged to preserve consumer[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpectations.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preservation of Critical Logic[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The existing pointer increments [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`in += …`, `out += …`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, return code [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ret`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand updates to `*inlen`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`*outlen` are untouched.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The early `break` on insufficient space yields `XML_ENC_ERR_SPACE`, matching [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe previous error-flow contract.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes are made to caller-side code [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `xmlEncInputChunk` or the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing harness[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Avoiding Side Effects[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By guarding each write against the original `*outlen` capacity, the fix [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensures no overflow while preserving successful conversions when space permits.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Performance impact is minimal: a few pointer subtractions per branch.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No broad exception/error catches are added.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No utility or harness code changes are needed.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification and References[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Explicit per-case guards follow the same pattern used elsewhere in libxml2’s [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mencoding conversions.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Balancing or removing the comment ensures the compiler no longer sees stray [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`*[0m[35m/[0m[39m`.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach directly addresses the AddressSanitizer overflow and the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstray-comment compilation error in one coherent patch.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Validation[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Compile the patched `encoding.c` to confirm the stray-comment error is [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolved.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run existing HTML fuzzing harness; confirm no heap-buffer-overflow in [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`UTF32ToUTF8`.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure all existing tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXML, HTML, encoding suites[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m pass without [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodifications. [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
